==== Ilias 24 ====
(1) λῦτο(Aor)(Med) δʼ(Pt) ἀγών(N), λαοὶ(N) δὲ(Pt) θοὰς(Adj)(A) ἐπὶ(Prp) νῆας(A) ἕκαστοι(Adj)(N)
(1) löste|sich aber Wettkampf, Leute aber schnelle zu Schiffe je|einzelne
(1) was|loosed but assembly, peoples but swift to ships each

(2) zerstreuten|sich zu|gehen. die|einen zwar des|Abendessens dachten|an
(2) were|scattering to|go. those indeed of|supper were|caring

(3) des|Schlafes auch süßen sich|zu|erfreuen· aber Achilleus
(3) of|sleep and sweet to|be|satisfied· but Achilleus

(6) of|Patroklos longing manhood and also might goodly,

(8) of|men and wars grievous and waves passing|through·

(10) at|another|time on sides lying|down, another|time but again
